INC-SPECT  Proton beam at the high resolution system. Absolute    F0918001   12

DETECTOR   (SIBAR) The first experiment was performed with five   F0918001   22 
           Si surface barrier detectors at laboratory angles of   F0918001   23 
           90, 108, 135, 150, and 165 degr.                       F0918001   24 
           In the second experiment transmission detectors were   F0918001   25 
           used to distinguish the alpha1 group from protons; the F0918001   26 
           detectors cleanly separated the proton and alpha peaks F0918001   27 
           for beam energies above 2.3 MeV. The final data were   F0918001   28 
           obtained with four surface barrier detectors at 90,    F0918001   29 
           125, 145, and 165 degr. and three transmission         F0918001   30 
           detectors at 105, 120, and 150 degr. Solid angles of   F0918001   31 
           the surface barrier detectors were adjusted such that  F0918001   32 
           the Rutherford scattering count rate was approximately F0918001   33 
           the same for all detectors.                            F0918001   34 
SAMPLE     Targets consisted of 1-3 ug/cm2 of Na. The vacuum      F0918001   35 
           evaporation was performed with sodium trititanate      F0918001   36 
            (Na2Ti3O7) in an open tantalum boat. Very little      F0918001   37 
           titanium was observed on the targets. The sodium was   F0918001   38 
           evaporated onto gold coated (~ 1 ug/cm2) carbon foils  F0918001   39 
            (~ 5 ug/cm2).                                         F0918001   40
